[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer run on the Mongoose HTTP library’s fuzz target detected a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte stack-buffer overflow in the floating-point formatting path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfunctions in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/printf.c and src/fmt.c invoked by mg_vxprintf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow occurs when [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprinting scientific notation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m‘%e’[0m[35m/[0m[39m‘%E’[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where a local buffer named `tmp` of size [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m is not large enough for certain inputs.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch was attempted that increases the temporary buffer sizes from [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m bytes,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madds default precision handling, clamps the requested precision to the buffer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapacity, and adjusts calls to `mg_dtoa` and related formatting functions. This [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was applied in three source files: src/fmt.c, src/mongoose.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe amalgamated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and a test file patched_mongoose.c.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, the build failed with C compilation errors in src/fmt.c: [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundeclared identifier `c`, mismatched braces, and unexpected tokens, indicating [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat the patch introduced syntactic issues.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer log shows an AddressSanitizer “stack-buffer-overflow” in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcalled from `mg_putchar_iobuf_static`, `scpy`, and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately `mg_vxprintf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow happens because, inside the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` handling in `mg_vxprintf` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mfmt.c: around line [0m[1;36m247[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and its counterpart in the amalgamated mongoose.c, a local[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray named `tmp` of fixed size [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m is written beyond its bounds when formatting [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertain double values.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer frame report pinpoints that writing a single byte at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverruns the second object [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tmp371`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the stack frame of `mg_vxprintf`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerable code path is specific to scientific-notation formatting [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m'e'[0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer-backed libFuzzer run on the Mongoose code uncovered a one-byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack buffer overflow inside the formatted-output machinery [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mg_pfn_iobuf_private`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ `mg_vxprintf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow occurs when handling floating-point conversion [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, writing past a small stack buffer. A community patch tried [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto enlarge the temporary buffer and adjust precision handling in both `src/fmt.c` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `mongoose.c`, but applying it broke the code’s control-flow and scoping: the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiler emitted a cascade of syntax errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmissing declarations, unbalanced [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbraces, unknown identifiers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the build failed entirely.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A fuzzing session with AddressSanitizer reported a stack-buffer-overflow in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_pfn_iobuf_private`, invoked by `mg_vxprintf` in `src/fmt.c`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The crash stack trace shows the overflow at an offset of [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m bytes into the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` stack frame, specifically overrunning a local array named `tmp371`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Two local buffers in `mg_vxprintf` were laid out as `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`; the write at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m just past the second buffer’s end.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error is triggered when `mg_log` calls `mg_http_parse`, which eventually [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformats floating-point values under `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E`, overflowing the small stack buffer. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The contributor edited the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` branch in `src/fmt.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m314[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplacing a fixed `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` with `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, adding default and clamped [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision logic, and splitting the exponent printing into two calls.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A mirrored change was grafted into `mongoose.c`’s `mg_vxprintf` block, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mre-implementing the `%e` code path there.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch added precision checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpr == [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m~0U[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer-size clamps [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpr > [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, calls to `mg_dtoa` with buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize, and additional writes via `[0m[1;35mout[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, param[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; n++;`.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Results  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On rebuild, the compiler immediately flagged syntax errors in `src/fmt.c`:  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • A non-void function path without a return.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `expected unqualified-id` at lines starting with `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msignaling brace or indentation mismatches.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Undeclared identifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ap`, `fmt`, `i`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and stray declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pr = [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m appearing outside any function scope.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Extraneous closing braces and misnested control structures.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The errors indicate the patch disrupted the original function structure, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperhaps by inserting code at incorrect indentation levels or without preserving the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrounding `while/if` scaffolding.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The build aborted with over [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m errors, so no executable was produced.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
